ACTOR Patchouli 31170
{
//This seems crazy but it's actually pretty practical
//Since I have to use ACS Anyway...
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
  Speed 7
  fastspeed 9
  MONSTER
  Health 1900
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 10000
  MinMissileChance 160
  //MinMissileChance 3000 //Geez this guy's coding was mental
  //MeleeThreshold 35 //ELE-MENTAL
  //MeleeRange 65 //GET IT?
  Species SDM
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +BOSS
  +DONTFALL
  +LOWGRAVITY
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +AMBUSH
  +NOICEDEATH
  Painchance 10
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Seesound ""
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  Obituary "%o failed to survive patchouli's elemental magic."
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	PTCH A 0
    PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,20,2,false)
	PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,20,30)
  Idle:
    PTCH BCDEFGHIJKLMA 2 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	PTCH A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    PTCH ABCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    PTCH P 15 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
	PTCH O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",70,"ProjectileAttack")
	PTCH M 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
	PTCH MMMMMMMMMMMMMM 1 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH M 1 A_SetAngle(angle+20)
    PTCH P 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/laser")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"blue","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyBlueLaserTrail",-8)

	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"blue","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",270,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyBlueLaserTrail",-8)
	PTCH O 1 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+2)
	PTCH O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",35,"SwitchSides")
	PTCH O 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH O 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	Goto Missile+17
  SwitchSides:
	PTCH O 0 A_FaceTarget

    PTCH O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/laser")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"blue","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyBlueLaserTrail",-8)

ACTOR PatchyBlueLaserTrail
{
  Radius 1
  Height 1
  RenderStyle Add
  Alpha 0.9
  XScale 0.4
  YScale 0.4
  +NoInteraction
  +ClientSideOnly
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    BLBL AB 2 Bright A_FadeOut(0.4)
    Loop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliNS2
{
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Speed 7
  fastspeed 9
  MONSTER
  Health 1900
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 10000
  MinMissileChance 160
  Species SDM
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +BOSS
  +DONTFALL
  +LOWGRAVITY
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +NOPAIN
  +AMBUSH
  Painchance 10
  Seesound ""
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  Obituary "%o failed to survive patchouli's elemental magic."
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",1,"Idle")
    PTCH A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.075)
    PTCH B 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.150)
    PTCH C 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.225)
    PTCH D 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.300)
    PTCH E 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.375)
    PTCH F 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.450)
    PTCH G 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.525)
    PTCH H 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.600)
    PTCH I 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.675)
    PTCH J 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.750)
    PTCH K 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.875)
    PTCH L 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.950)
    PTCH M 2 A_SetTranslucent(1.000)
    Goto Idle
  Idle:
    PTCH ABCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6023)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6023,1,false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6023,30)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter2",1)
	PTCH M 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    PTCH ABCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    PTCH P 15 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
	PTCH M 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
	PTCH O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",70,"ProjectileAttack")
	PTCH MMMMMMMMMMMMMM 1 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH M 1 A_SetAngle(angle-20)
    PTCH P 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/laser")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",90,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",180,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",270,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	PTCH O 1 Bright A_SetAngle(angle-2)
	PTCH O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",35,"SwitchSides")
	PTCH O 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH O 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	Goto Missile+17
  SwitchSides:
	PTCH O 0 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH O 0 A_SetAngle(angle+20)
    PTCH O 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/laser")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",0,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",90,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",180,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(10,0,"red","white",RGF_SILENT|RGF_FULLBRIGHT|RGF_EXPLICITANGLE,0,0,"BulletPuff",270,0,0,0,6.0,0,"PatchyRedLaserTrail")
	PTCH O 1 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+2)
	PTCH O 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",70,"See")
	PTCH O 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH O 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	Goto SwitchSides+3
  ProjectileAttack:

ACTOR PatchouliRedOrb
{
  Radius 5
  Speed 16
  fastspeed 24
  Height 10
  damage (15)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  DamageType "SDM"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RBL1 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    RBL1 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliSpellcard //31172
{
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Speed 7
  fastspeed 9
  MONSTER
  Health 1800
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 10000
  MinMissileChance 160
  Species SDM
  +NOPAIN
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +BOSS
  +DONTFALL
  +LOWGRAVITY
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +AMBUSH
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +NOICEDEATH
  Painchance 5
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Seesound ""
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  Obituary "%o failed to survive patchouli's elemental magic."
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",1,"Idle")
    PTCH A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.075)
    PTCH B 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.150)
    PTCH C 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.225)
    PTCH D 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.300)
    PTCH E 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.375)
    PTCH F 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.450)
    PTCH G 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.525)
    PTCH H 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.600)
    PTCH I 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.675)
    PTCH J 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.750)
    PTCH K 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.875)
    PTCH L 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.950)
    PTCH M 2 A_SetTranslucent(1.000)
    Goto Idle
  Idle:
    PTCH ABCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",1,"ChaseState")
    PTCH A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH Q 6 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH Q 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	PTCH RSRSRSRSRS 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	PTCH A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    PTCH ABCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    PTCH P 15 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
  Missile:
  SpellcardAttack:
    PTCH A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("UltraMode",1,"SpellcardUltra")
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"SpellcardLunatic")
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"SpellcardHard")
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"SpellcardNormal")
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"SpellcardEasy")
	Goto SpellcardHard
  SpellcardEasy:
  SpellcardNormal:
  SpellcardHard:
  SpellcardLunatic:
  SpellcardUltra:
    Goto See
  Death:
	PTCH A 0 A_NoBlocking
	PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
/*
    PTCH Q 35
	PTCH Q 0 A_NoBlocking
    PTCH Q 0 A_scream
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
*/
	PTCH A 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
	PTCH A 0 ACS_Execute(603)
	PTCH A 0 ACS_Execute(604,0,2)
    PTCH BCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_FadeOut
    Stop
  DeathExplosion:
	PTCH P 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	PTCH P 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	PTCH P 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
    PTCH P 0 ACS_Execute(603)
	PTCH P 35
	PTCH P 0 A_NoBlocking
    PTCH P 0 A_Scream
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	Stop
  }
}
ACTOR PatchouliSpellcard2 : PatchouliSpellcard //31172
{
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
  Health 2000
  States
  {
  Death:
	PTCH A 0 A_NoBlocking
	PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	PTCH A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
/*
    PTCH Q 35
	PTCH Q 0 A_NoBlocking
    PTCH Q 0 A_scream
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
*/
	PTCH A 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
	PTCH A 0 ACS_Execute(603)
	PTCH A 0 ACS_Execute(604,0,4)
    PTCH BCDEFGHIJKLM 2 A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}
//And here's why I did things the way I did.
//There are a lot of different spellcards, and Patchy won't use all of them.
//Not in one fight, anyway.
//And doing seperate Patchy fights for different combinations,
//each thousands of lines of code...yeah, no.
ACTOR PatchouliAgniShine : PatchouliSpellcard
{
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
  PainChance 1
  States
  {
  See:
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",1,"ChaseState")
    PTCH A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH Q 6 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6024)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6024,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_PatchouliSpellCardsLeft",0),true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6024,35)
	PTCH Q 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,11)
	PTCH Q 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	PTCH RSRSRSRSRS 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto SpellcardAttack
  SpellcardEasy:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter4",72,"ReverseDirectionEasy")
	PTCH UUUU 0 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))
	PTCH U 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))
	PTCH VVVV 0 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))
	PTCH V 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))
	PTCH V 0 A_SetAngle(angle+10)
	PTCH V 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter4",1)
	PTCH V 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter4",72,"See")
	PTCH V 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	Goto SpellcardEasy+1
  ReverseDirectionEasy:
	PTCH T 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter4",200)
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH UUUU 0 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))

	PTCH V 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-15,15),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,15))

	PTCH U 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-20,20),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,18))
	PTCH VVVVVV 0 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-20,20),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,18))
	PTCH V 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-20,20),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,18))
	PTCH V 0 A_SetAngle(angle+10)

	PTCH V 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter4",72,"ReverseDirectionNormal")
	PTCH V 0 A_CheckSight("See")
	Goto SpellcardNormal+1
  ReverseDirectionNormal:

	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget

	PTCH U 1 A_CustomMissile("PatchouliAgniShineOrb",frandom(16,48),0,frandom(-20,20),CMF_AIMDIRECTION,frandom(-15,18))

ACTOR PatchouliRageTrilithonOrb
{
  Radius 4
  Speed 12
  fastspeed 10
  Height 8
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	YBL2 A 0
    YBL2 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	YBL2 AAAA 4 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(0.5)
	YBL2 A 0 Bright A_Stop
	YBL2 A 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+frandom(-90,90))
	YBL2 AA 4 Bright ThrustThing(angle*256/360, 8, 0, 0)
  LoopState:
    YBL2 A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
	YBL2 AAAAAAAAAA 1 A_FadeOut
	Stop
  }
}
ACTOR PatchouliRageTrilithonOrbAimed
{
  Radius 10
  Speed 18
  fastspeed 25
  Height 20
  damage (30)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    YBUB A 1 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    YBUB AAAAAAAAAA 2 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliForestBlazeOrb
{
  Radius 3
  Speed 20
  fastspeed 30
  Height 6
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  RenderStyle add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  DamageType "SDM"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_ScaleVelocity(frandom(0.4,1.25))
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(170,"LoopYellow","LoopRed")
  LoopGreen:
    GRIC A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  LoopYellow:
    YRIC A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  LoopRed:
    RRIC A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  Death:
    "####" AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliWaterElfOrbGreen
{
  Radius 6
  Speed 16
  fastspeed 24
  Height 12
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  //RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  DamageType "SDM"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    GBL1 A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
    GBL1 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliMercuryPoisonOrbYellow1
{
  Radius 6
  Speed 14
  fastspeed 24
  Height 12
  damage (10)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  //RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit2"
  DamageType "SDM"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    YBL1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	YBL1 A 0 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(0.96)
	YBL1 A 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+4)
	YBL1 A 4 Bright ThrustThing(angle*256/360, 1, 0, 0)
    Loop
  Death:
    YBL1 AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR PatchouliEmeraldMegalith : PatchouliSpellcard2
{
  Tag "Patchouli Knowledge"
  States
  {
  See:
    PTCH A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1",1,"ChaseState")
    PTCH A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1",1)
	PTCH Q 6 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6033)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6033,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6033,40)
	PTCH Q 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,20)
	PTCH Q 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1,0,ATTN_NONE)
	PTCH RSRSRSRSRS 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto SpellcardAttack
  SpellcardEasy:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 7 A_CustomMissile("EmeraldMegalithOrbSpawnerEasy",frandom(20,40),frandom(256,-256),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	PTCH V 7 A_SpidRefire
	Goto SpellcardEasy+1
  SpellcardNormal:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 7 A_CustomMissile("EmeraldMegalithOrbSpawnerNormal",frandom(20,40),frandom(256,-256),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	PTCH V 7 A_SpidRefire
	Goto SpellcardNormal+1
  SpellcardHard:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 7 A_CustomMissile("EmeraldMegalithOrbSpawnerHard",frandom(20,40),frandom(256,-256),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	PTCH V 7 A_SpidRefire
	Goto SpellcardHard+1
  SpellcardLunatic:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 7 A_CustomMissile("EmeraldMegalithOrbSpawnerLunatic",frandom(20,40),frandom(320,-320),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	PTCH V 7 A_SpidRefire
	Goto SpellcardLunatic+1
  SpellcardUltra:
	PTCH T 14 A_FaceTarget
	PTCH U 7 A_CustomMissile("EmeraldMegalithOrbSpawnerUltra",frandom(20,40),frandom(384,-384),0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	PTCH V 7 A_SpidRefire
	Goto SpellcardLunatic+1
  }
}

I've since given up on that, but I'm keeping the code here for old times' sake.

the references to this, so it has to stay in to make sure nothing blows up.

actor LascannonBurst
{
    +PUFFGETSOWNER    
    +SERVERSIDEONLY
    +FORCERADIUSDMG
	
    Radius 6
    Height 6

    Obituary "%k vaporised %o."

    States
    {
      Spawn:
        TNT1 A 0
        TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(800, 160, 0)
        stop
    }
}

        stop
    }
}
